*bus, unsigned int val);\n707: /*\n708:  * Interface for HD codec\n709:  */\n710: \n711: /*\n712:  * CORB / RIRB interface\n713:  */\n714: static int azx_alloc_cmd_io(struct azx *chip)\n715: {\n716: \tmark_pages_wc(chip, &chip->rb, true);\n727: \treturn 0;\n728: }\n729: \n730: static void azx_init_cmd_io(struct azx *chip)\n731: {\n732: \tspin_lock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n733: \t/* CORB set up */\n734: \tchip->corb.addr = chip->rb.addr;\n735: \tchip->corb.buf = (u32 *)chip->rb.area;\n736: \tazx_writel(chip, CORBLBASE, (u32)chip->corb.addr);\n737: \tazx_writel(chip, CORBUBASE, upper_32_bits(chip->corb.addr));\n738: \n739: \t/* set the corb size to 256 entries (ULI requires explicitly) */\n740: \tazx_writeb(chip, CORBSIZE, 0x02);\n741: \t/* set the corb write pointer to 0 */\n742: \tazx_writew(chip, CORBWP, 0);\n743: \t/* reset the corb hw read pointer */\n744: \tazx_writew(chip, CORBRP, ICH6_CORBRP_RST);\n745: \t/* enable corb dma */\n746: \tazx_writeb(chip, CORBCTL, ICH6_CORBCTL_RUN);\n747: \n748: \t/* RIRB set up */\n749: \tchip->rirb.addr = chip->rb.addr + 2048;\n750: \tchip->rirb.buf = (u32 *)(chip->rb.area + 2048);\n751: \tchip->rirb.wp = chip->rirb.rp = 0;\n752: \tmemset(chip->rirb.cmds, 0, sizeof(chip->rirb.cmds));\n753: \tazx_writel(chip, RIRBLBASE, (u32)chip->rirb.addr);\n754: \tazx_writel(chip, RIRBUBASE, upper_32_bits(chip->rirb.addr));\n755: \n756: \t/* set the rirb size to 256 entries (ULI requires explicitly) */\n757: \tazx_writeb(chip, RIRBSIZE, 0x02);\n758: \t/* reset the rirb hw write pointer */\n759: \tazx_writew(chip, RIRBWP, ICH6_RIRBWP_RST);\n760: \t/* set N=1, get RIRB response interrupt for new entry */\n761: \tif (chip->driver_caps & AZX_DCAPS_CTX_WORKAROUND)\n762: \t\tazx_writew(chip, RINTCNT, 0xc0);\n763: \telse\n764: \t\tazx_writew(chip, RINTCNT, 1);\n765: \t/* enable rirb dma and response irq */\n766: \tazx_writeb(chip, RIRBCTL, ICH6_RBCTL_DMA_EN | ICH6_RBCTL_IRQ_EN);\n767: \tspin_unlock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n768: }\n769: \n770: static void azx_free_cmd_io(struct azx *chip)\n771: {\n772: \tspin_lock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n773: \t/* disable ringbuffer DMAs */\n774: \tazx_writeb(chip, RIRBCTL, 0);\n775: \tazx_writeb(chip, CORBCTL, 0);\n776: \tspin_unlock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n777: }\n778: \n779: static unsigned int azx_command_addr(u32 cmd)\n780: {\n781: \tunsigned int addr = cmd >> 28;\n782: \n783: \tif (addr >= AZX_MAX_CODECS) {\n784: \t\tsnd_BUG();\n785: \t\taddr = 0;\n786: \t}\n787: \n788: \treturn addr;\n789: }\n790: \n791: static unsigned int azx_command_addr(val);\n808: \tunsigned int wp;\n809: \n810: \tspin_lock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n811: \n812: \t/* add command to corb */\n813: \twp = azx_readb(chip, CORBWP);\n814: \twp++;\n815: \twp %= ICH6_MAX_CORB_ENTRIES;\n816: \n817: \tchip->rirb.cmds[addr]++;\n818: \tchip->corb.buf[wp] = cpu_to_le32(val);\n819: \tazx_writel(chip, CORBWP, wp);\n820: \n821: \tspin_unlock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n822: \n823: \treturn 0;\n824: }\n825: \n826: #define ICH6_RIRB_EX_UNSOL_EV\t(1<<4)\n827: \n828: /* retrieve RIRB entry - called from interrupt handler */\n829: static void azx_update_rirb(struct azx *chip)\n830: {\n831: \tunsigned int rp, wp;\n832: \tunsigned int addr;\n833: \tu32 res, res_ex;\n834: \n835: \twp = azx_readb(chip, RIRBWP);\n836: \tif (wp == chip->rirb.wp)\n837: \t\treturn;\n838: \tchip->rirb.wp = wp;\n839: \n840: \twhile (chip->rirb.rp != wp) {\n841: \t\tchip->rirb.rp++;\n842: \t\tchip->rirb.rp %= ICH6_MAX_RIRB_ENTRIES;\n843: \n844: \t\trp = chip->rirb.rp << 1; /* an RIRB entry is 8-bytes */\n845: \t\tres_ex = le32_to_cpu(chip->rirb.buf[rp + 1]);\n846: \t\tres = le32_to_cpu(chip->rirb.buf[rp]);\n847: \t\taddr = azx_response_addr(res_ex);\n848: \t\tif (res_ex & ICH6_RIRB_EX_UNSOL_EV)\n849: \t\t\tsnd_hda_queue_unsol_event(chip->bus, res, res_ex);\n850: \t\telse if (chip->rirb.cmds[addr]) {\n851: \t\t\tchip->rirb.res[addr] = res;\n852: \t\t\tsmp_wmb();\n853: \t\t\tchip->rirb.cmds[addr]--;\n854: \t\t} else\n855: \t\t\tsnd_printk(KERN_ERR SFX \"spurious response %#x:%#x, \"\n856: \t\t\t\t   \"last cmd=%#08x\\n\",\n857: \t\t\t\t   res, res_ex,\n858: \t\t\t\t   chip->last_cmd[addr]);\n859: \t}\n860: }\n861: \n862: /* receive a response */\n863: static unsigned int azx_rirb_get_response(struct hda_bus *bus,\n864: \t\t\t\t\t  unsigned int addr)\n865: {\n866: \tstruct azx *chip = bus->private_data;\n867: \tunsigned long timeout;\n868: \tunsigned long || do_poll) {\n876: \t\t\tspin_lock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n877: \t\t\tazx_update_rirb(chip);\n878: \t\t\tspin_unlock_irq(&chip->reg_lock);\n879: \t\t}\n880: \t\tif (!chip->rirb.cmds[addr]) {\n881: \t\t\tsmp_rmb();\n882: \t\t\tbus->rirb_error = 0;\n883: \n884: \t\t\tif (!do_poll)\n885: \t\t\t\tchip->poll_count = 0;\n886: \t\t\treturn chip->rirb.res[addr]; /* the last value */\n887: \t\t}\n888: \t\tif (time_after(jiffies, timeout))\n889: \t\t\tbreak;\n890: \t\tif (bus->needs_damn_long_delay || loopcounter > 3000)\n891: \t\t\tmsleep(2); /* temporary workaround */\n892: \t\telse {\n893: \t\t\tudelay(10);\n894: \t\t\tcond_resched();\n895: \t\t}\n896: \t}\n897: \n898: \tif (!chip->polling_mode && chip->poll_count < 2) {\n899: \t\tsnd_printdd(SFX \"azx_get_response timeout, \"\n900: \t\t\t   \"polling the codec once: last cmd=0x%08x\\n\",\n901: \t\t\t   chip->last_cmd[addr]);\n902: \t\tdo_poll = 1;\n903: \t\tchip->poll_count++;\n904: \t\tgoto again;\n905: \t}\n906: \n907: \n908: \tif (!chip->polling_mode) {\n909: \t\tsnd_printk(KERN_WARNING SFX \"azx_get_response timeout, \"\n910: \t\t\t   \"switching to polling mode: last cmd=0x%08x\\n\",\n911: \t\t\t   chip->last_cmd[addr]);\n912: \t\tchip->polling_mode = 1;\n913: \t\tgoto again;\n914: \t}\n915: \n916: \tif (chip->msi) {\n917: \t\tsnd_printk(KERN_WARNING SFX \"No response from codec, \"\n918: \t\t\t   \"disabling MSI: last cmd=0x%08x\\n\",\n919: \t\t\t   chip->last_cmd[addr]);\n920: \t\tfree_irq(chip->irq, chip);\n921: \t\tchip->irq = -1;\n922: \t\tpci_disable_msi(chip->pci);\n923: \t\tchip->msi = 0;\n924: \t\tif (azx_acquire_irq(chip, 1) < 0) {\n925: \t\t\tbus->rirb_error = 1;\n926: \t\t\treturn -1;\n927: \t\t}\n928: \t\tgoto again;\n929: \t}\n930: \n931: \tif (chip->probing) {\n932: \t\t/* If this critical timeout happens during the codec probing\n933: \t\t * phase, this is likely an access to a non-existing codec\n934: \t\t * slot.  Better to return an error and reset the system.\n935: \t\t */\n936: \t\treturn -1;\n937: \t}\n938: \n939: \t/* a fatal communication error; need either to reset or to fallback\n940: \t * to the single_cmd mode\n941: \t */\n942: \tbus->rirb_error = 1;\n943: \tif (bus->allow_bus_reset && !bus->response_reset && !bus->in_reset) {\n944: \t\tbus->response_reset = 1;\n945: \t\treturn -1; /* give a chance to retry */\n946: \t}\n947: \n948: \tsnd_printk(KERN_ERR \"hda_intel: azx_get_response timeout, \"\n949: \t\t   \"switching to single_cmd mode: last cmd=0x%08x\\n\",\n950: \t\t   chip->last_cmd[addr]);\n951: \tchip->single_cmd = 1;\n952: \tbus->response_reset = 0;\n953: \t/* release CORB/RIRB */\n954: \tazx_free_cmd_io(chip);\n955: \t/* disable unsolicited responses */\n956: \tazx_writel(chip, GCTL, azx_readl(chip, GCTL) & ~ICH6_GCTL_UNSOL);\n957: \treturn -1;\n958: }\n959: \n960: /*\n961:  * Use the single immediate command instead of CORB/RIRB for simplicity\n962:  *\n963:  * Note: according to Intel, this is not preferred use.  The command was\n964:  *       intended for the BIOS only, and may get confused with unsolicited\n965:  *       responses.  So, we shouldn't use it for normal operation from the\n966:  *       driver.\n967:  *       I left the codes, however, for debugging/testing purposes.\n968:  */\n969: \n970: /* receive a response */\n971: static int azx_single_wait_for_response(struct azx *chip, unsigned int addr)\n972: {\n973: \tint timeout = 50;\n974: \n975: \twhile (timeout--) {\n976: \t\t/* check IRV busy bit */\n977: \t\tif (azx_readw(chip, IRS) & ICH6_IRS_VALID) {\n978: \t\t\t/* reuse rirb.res as the response return value */\n979: \t\t\tchip->rirb.res[addr] = azx_readl(chip, IR);\n980: \t\t\treturn 0;\n981: \t\t}\n982: \t\tudelay(1);\n983: \t}\n984: \tif (printk_ratelimit())\n985: \t\tsnd_printd(SFX \"get_response timeout: IRS=0x%x\\n\",\n986: \t\t\t   azx_readw(chip, IRS));\n987: \tchip->rirb.res[addr] = -1;\n988: \treturn -EIO;\n989: }\n990: \n991: /* send a command */\n992: static int azx_single_send_cmd(struct hda_bus *bus, u32 val)\n993: {\n994: \tstruct azx *chip = bus->private_data;\n995: \tunsigned int addr = azx_command_addr(val);\n996: \tint timeout = 50;\n997: \n998: \tbus->rirb_error = 0;\n999: \twhile (timeout--) {\n1000: \t\t/* check ICB busy bit */\n1001: \t\tif azx_power_notify(struct hda_bus *bus, bool power_up);\n1062: #endif\n1063: \n1064: /* reset codec link */\n1065: static int azx_reset(struct azx *chip, int full_reset)\n1066: {\n1067: \tint SD_CTL_STREAM_RESET);\n1498: \tudelay(3);\n1499: \ttimeout = 300;\n1500: \twhile (!((val = azx_sd_readb(azx_dev, SD_CTL)) & SD_CTL_STREAM_RESET) &&\n1501: \t       --timeout)\n1502: \t\t;\n1503: \tval */\n1509: \twhile (((val = azx_sd_readb(azx_dev, SD_CTL)) & SD_CTL_STREAM_RESET) &&\n1510: \t       --timeout)\n1511: \t\t;\n1512: \n1513: \t/* reset first position - may not be synced with hw at this time */\n1514: \t*azx_dev->posbuf = 0;\n1515: }\n1516: \n1517: /*\n1518:  * set up the SD for streaming\n1519:  */\n1520: static int azx_setup_controller(struct azx *chip, struct azx_dev *azx_dev)\n1521: {\n1522: \tunsigned int val;\n1523: \t/* make sure the run bit is zero for SD */\n1524: \tazx_stream_clear(chip, azx_dev);\n1525: \t/* program the stream_tag */\n1526: \tval = azx_sd_readl(azx_dev, SD_CTL);\n1527: \tval = (val & ~SD_CTL_STREAM_TAG_MASK) |\n1528: \t\t(azx_dev->stream_tag << SD_CTL_STREAM_TAG_SHIFT);\n1529: \tif (!azx_snoop(chip))\n1530: \t\tval |= azx_dev->bufsize);\n1535: \n1536: \t/* program the stream format */\n1537: \t/* this value needs to be the same as the one programmed */\n1538: \tazx_sd_writew(azx_dev, SD_FORMAT, azx_dev->format_val);\n1539: \n1540: \t/* program the stream LVI (last valid index) of the BDL */\n1541: \tazx_sd_writew(azx_dev, SD_LVI, azx_dev->frags - 1);\n1542: \n1543: \t/* program the BDL address */\n1544: \t/* lower BDL address */\n1545: \tazx_sd_writel(azx_dev, SD_BDLPL, (u32)azx_dev->bdl.addr);\n1546: \t/* upper BDL address */\n1547: \tazx_sd_writel(azx_dev, SD_BDLPU, upper_32_bits(azx_dev->bdl.addr));\n1548: \n1549: \t/* enable the position buffer */\n1550: \tif (chip->position_fix[0] != POS_FIX_LPIB ||\n1551: \t    chip->position_fix[1] != POS_FIX_LPIB) {\n1552: \t\tif (!(azx_readl(chip, DPLBASE) & ICH6_DPLBASE_ENABLE))\n1553: \t\t\tazx_writel(chip, DPLBASE,\n1554: \t\t\t\t(u32)chip->posbuf.addr | ICH6_DPLBASE_ENABLE);\n1555: \t}\n1556: \n1557: \t/* set the interrupt enable bits in the descriptor control register */\n1558: \tazx_sd_writel(azx_dev, SD_CTL,\n1559: \t\t      azx_sd_readl(azx_dev, SD_CTL) | SD_INT_MASK);\n1560: \n1561: \treturn 0;\n1562: }\n1563: \n1564: /*\n1565:  * Probe the given codec address\n1566:  */\n1567: static int probe_codec(struct azx *chip, int addr)\n1568: {\n1569: \tunsigned int cmd = (addr << 28) | (AC_NODE_ROOT << \t\t\t\t struct hda_pcm *cpcm);\n1587: static void azx_stop_chip(struct azx *chip);\n1588: \n1589: static void azx_bus_reset(struct hda_bus *bus)\n1590: {\n1591: \tstruct azx *chip = So when resume tries to re-enable MSI, it assumes the flag reflects the actual hardware state, when it doesn't. The mismatch between the flag and actual MSI state could cause the IRQ acquisition to fail or behave unexpectedly.\n\nLooking at the resume sequence, it's missing a critical step that happens during initial probe—MSI needs to be re-enabled before acquiring the IRQ, but the current code doesn't guarantee this ordering. The flag gets checked, MSI gets enabled if the flag is set, but if that fails silently or if there's a state mismatch, the IRQ setup downstream could be working with the wrong interrupt type.\n\nThe actual failure manifests when a codec command times out after resume. The driver retries with polling mode, but if MSI is in an inconsistent state (disabled in hardware but the driver thinks it's enabled), the interrupt handler won't fire properly, causing the timeout. Only after multiple retries does it finally disable MSI in software as a fallback.\n\nThis suggests the codec communication itself is broken post-resume. I should check what changed in v3.7.1 around suspend/resume handling, particularly whether azx_init_chip's full_reset parameter might be disabling something critical that needs to stay {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_011M7wMbXpPQwu9QEwZJUjbe","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I can see the difference clearly. Init chip with full_reset=1 (2561)\n8. Resume codec bus (2563)\n\nThe missing line is synchronize_irq! This is probably the bug. After acquiring a new IRQ during resume, we need to synchronize_irq to ensure any pending interrupts from before are cleared.\n\nBut wait, let me think about this more. If polling_mode or single_cmd mode is triggered during the resume, it means that the codec communication is failing. If synchronize_irq was missing, it might cause the IRQ handler to be in a bad state, causing the codec to not respond.\n\nActually, I think there's another issue. Looking at the code more carefully, I notice that during initial probe, synchronize_irq is called AFTER pci_set_master. But in azx_resume, there's no synchronize_irq at all.\n\nThis could definitely be the cause of the bug. After resume, if there are any pending interrupts from before suspend, they won't be synchronized, potentially causing the IRQ handler to be out of sync with the hardware state.\n\nAlso, I notice another potential issue. In azx_resume, azx_init_pci is called AFTER azx_acquire_irq, whereas in azx_first_init, it reads GCAP register AFTER synchronize_irq (indirectly, the hardware initialization happens later). But this is probably not the main issue.\n\n\nI should also check whether polling_mode and single_cmd flags persist across suspend/resume cycles. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01VymvhSTfQmy1V7X7E5jrW3","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"thinking","thinking":"Now I have a pretty good picture. Let me summarize what I've found:\n\nThe bug is in the azx_resume function (line 2539-2566). Comparing it to azx_first_init, the missing elements are:1. synchronize_irq(chip->irq) - This is called in azx_first_init at line 3159, but missing in azx_resume2. Reset of chip->polling_mode and chip->single_cmd flags - These should be reset to 0 before resuming The missing synchronize_irq is likely the primary issue. After suspending the device and freeing the IRQ, when we request a new IRQ during resume, we need to synchronize it with the hardware to ensure any pending interrupts are cleared and the IRQ handler During resume:\n   - The PCI device is re-enabled\n   - MSI is re-enabled  \n   - A new IRQ is requested via `azx_acquire_irq()`\n   - **BUT**: The `synchronize_irq()` call that synchronizes the IRQ with hardware state is missing\n\n2. **Race Condition**: Without `synchronize_irq()`, there's a window where:\n   - The kernel's IRQ handler registration is out of sync with hardware state\n   - Any pending interrupts from before suspend aren't properly cleared\n   - The codec communication becomes unreliable\n\n3. **Stale State Flags**: Additionally, the `chip->polling_mode` and `chip->single_cmd` flags are not reset during resume, causing the system to remain in degraded modes if they were set before suspend.\n\n### Evidence\n- **azx_first_init** (line 3151-3159): Properly initializes with MSI, acquire_irq, set_master, **synchronize_irq**\n- **azx_resume** (line 2545-2561): Has MSI, acquire_irq, set_master, **BUT MISSING synchronize_irq**\n\n### Symptoms Explained\nThe missing synchronization causes:\n1. First codec communication after resume to timeout\n2. System falls back to polling mode\n3. Still times out, then disables MSI and re-acquires IRQ\n4. Eventually switches to single_cmd mode\n5.
